SET StubDirectory TO $'''C:\\edit\\this\\path'''
DateTime.GetCurrentDateTime.Local DateTimeFormat: DateTime.DateTimeFormat.DateAndTime CurrentDateTime=> CurrentDateTime
SET ErrorTracker TO $'''false'''
SET MonitorDirectory TO $'''C:\\edit\\this\\path'''
SET MonitorFile TO $'''monitor.txt'''
SET KeepRunning TO $'''true'''
LOOP WHILE (ErrorTracker) = ($'''false''')
    IF (System.IfProcess.ProcessIsRunning ProcessName: $'''bambu-studio''') THEN
        IF (System.IfProcess.ProcessIsRunning ProcessName: $'''ffplay''') THEN
            UIAutomation.GetElementDetails Element: appmask['Pane \'3x5_Drawer_FullSet - BambuStudio\'']['Text \'Finish Time: 02:29\''] AttributeName: $'''Own Text''' BringToFront: False AttributeValue=> FinishTime
            ON ERROR REPEAT 1 TIMES WAIT 2
            END
            IF FinishTime <> $'''Finished''' THEN
                UIAutomation.GetElementDetails Element: appmask['Pane \'3x5_Drawer_FullSet - BambuStudio\'']['Text \'Filament_Roller_v1\''] AttributeName: $'''Own Text''' BringToFront: False AttributeValue=> FileName
                ON ERROR REPEAT 1 TIMES WAIT 2
                ON ERROR
                    SET ErrorTracker TO $'''true'''
                END
                UIAutomation.GetElementDetails Element: appmask['Pane \'3x5_Drawer_FullSet - BambuStudio\'']['Text \'Layer: 1/182\''] AttributeName: $'''Own Text''' BringToFront: False AttributeValue=> Layers
                ON ERROR REPEAT 1 TIMES WAIT 2
                ON ERROR
                    SET ErrorTracker TO $'''true'''
                END
                UIAutomation.GetElementDetails Element: appmask['Pane \'3x5_Drawer_FullSet - BambuStudio\'']['Text \'-4h29m\''] AttributeName: $'''Own Text''' BringToFront: False AttributeValue=> RemainingTime
                ON ERROR
                    SET ErrorTracker TO $'''true'''
                END
                UIAutomation.GetElementDetails Element: appmask['Pane \'3x5_Drawer_FullSet - BambuStudio\'']['Text \'23m18s\''] AttributeName: $'''Own Text''' BringToFront: False AttributeValue=> TotalTime
                ON ERROR REPEAT 1 TIMES WAIT 2
                ON ERROR
                    SET ErrorTracker TO $'''true'''
                END
                UIAutomation.GetElementDetails Element: appmask['Pane \'3x5_Drawer_FullSet - BambuStudio\'']['Text \'11.17g\''] AttributeName: $'''Own Text''' BringToFront: False AttributeValue=> Filament
                ON ERROR REPEAT 1 TIMES WAIT 2
                ON ERROR
                    SET Errortracker TO $'''true'''
                END
                UIAutomation.GetElementDetails Element: appmask['Pane \'3x5_Drawer_FullSet - BambuStudio\'']['Text \'100\''] AttributeName: $'''Own Text''' BringToFront: False AttributeValue=> PercentComplete
                ON ERROR REPEAT 1 TIMES WAIT 2
                ON ERROR
                    SET ErrorTracker TO $'''true'''
                END
                UIAutomation.GetElementDetails Element: appmask['Pane \'3x5_Drawer_FullSet - BambuStudio\'']['Pane \'83\''] AttributeName: $'''Own Text''' BringToFront: False AttributeValue=> NozzleTemp
                ON ERROR REPEAT 1 TIMES WAIT 2
                ON ERROR
                    SET ErrorTracker TO $'''true'''
                END
                UIAutomation.GetElementDetails Element: appmask['Pane \'3x5_Drawer_FullSet - BambuStudio\'']['Pane \'64\' 2'] AttributeName: $'''Own Text''' BringToFront: False AttributeValue=> BedTemp
                ON ERROR REPEAT 1 TIMES WAIT 2
                ON ERROR
                    SET ErrorTracker TO $'''true'''
                END
                IF ErrorTracker = $'''false''' THEN
                    Text.Replace Text: FileName TextToFind: $'''%%%%''' IsRegEx: True IgnoreCase: False ReplaceWith: $'''\\%%''' ActivateEscapeSequences: False Result=> CleanFileName
                    Text.Replace Text: NozzleTemp TextToFind: $'''\\r\\n''' IsRegEx: True IgnoreCase: False ReplaceWith: $'''/''' ActivateEscapeSequences: False Result=> NozzletempFixed
                    Text.Replace Text: FileName TextToFind: $'''%%''' IsRegEx: False IgnoreCase: False ReplaceWith: $'''\\%%''' ActivateEscapeSequences: False Result=> CleanFileName
                    Text.Replace Text: BedTemp TextToFind: $'''\\r\\n''' IsRegEx: True IgnoreCase: False ReplaceWith: $'''/''' ActivateEscapeSequences: False Result=> BedTempFixed
                    SET ContentData TO $'''File: %CleanFileName%
Filament: %Filament%
Duration: %TotalTime%
Remaining: %RemainingTime% (%PercentComplete%\\%%)
%FinishTime%
%Layers%
Nozzle: %NozzleTempFixed% °C
Bed: %BedTempFixed% °C'''
                    Text.Replace Text: ContentData TextToFind: $'''\\r\\n''' IsRegEx: True IgnoreCase: False ReplaceWith: $'''\\n''' ActivateEscapeSequences: True Result=> FileContent
                    File.WriteText File: $'''%MonitorDirectory%\\%MonitorFile%''' TextToWrite: FileContent AppendNewLine: False IfFileExists: File.IfFileExists.Overwrite Encoding: File.FileEncoding.UTF8
                    ON ERROR

                    END
                    WAIT 20
                    SET ErrorTracker TO $'''false'''
                END
            ELSE
                File.WriteText File: $'''%MonitorDirectory%\\%MonitorFile%''' TextToWrite: FinishTime AppendNewLine: False IfFileExists: File.IfFileExists.Overwrite Encoding: File.FileEncoding.UTF8
                ON ERROR

                END
                WAIT 120
            END
        ELSE
            WAIT (System.WaitForProcess.ProcessToStart ProcessName: $'''ffplay''')
        END
    ELSE
        WAIT (System.WaitForProcess.ProcessToStart ProcessName: $'''bambu-studio''')
    END
END
